function rightRailPreviewPlayerPostProcessor (elements,model) {
if( window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isFlashInstalled()&&!window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isMobileClient()) {
var thumbChangeObserver = model.thumbnail.subscribe(function(newValue) {
if($j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").length>0) {
$j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").each(function(index){
$j(this).attr("src", newValue);
});
}
else {
if(thumbChangeObserver)thumbChangeObserver.dispose();
}
});
$j(elements).find(".tn").unbind("click");
var vidStreamUrl;
vidStreamUrl = 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr';
callCnnVideo({
key: 'rightRail',
preset: 'right-rail-preview',
markupid: 'nowPlayingThumbnail',
video: 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr',
placement: 'rightRail',
adsection: 'cnn.com_main_homepage_rightrail_muted',
headline: '',
width:'300',
height:'169',
source: 'CNN',
sourceUrl: '',
section: 'largevideo',
videoStreamUrl: vidStreamUrl
});
}
};

<!-- Visual Revenue script for blog and partner links -->
var all_links = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
for (var i = 0 ; i < all_links.length ; i++) {
var href = all_links[i].getAttribute('href');
if (!href || all_links[i].getAttribute('onclick')) continue;
var boolOnClick = true;
if (href.charAt(0) == "/") boolOnClick = false;
else if (href.indexOf("www.cnn.com") != -1 || href.indexOf("blogs.cnn.com") != -1 || href.indexOf("edition.cnn.com") != -1) boolOnClick = false;
if (boolOnClick == true) {
var cleanLink = href.split('&hpt=')[0].split('?hpt=')[0];
all_links[i].setAttribute('onclick', '_vrtrack({ track_url : \'' + cleanLink + '\' })');
}
}
<!-- End Visual Revenue script for blog and partner links -->

var thumbChangeObserver = model.thumbnail.subscribe(function(newValue) {
if($j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").length>0) {
$j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").each(function(index){
$j(this).attr("src", newValue);
});
}
else {
if(thumbChangeObserver)thumbChangeObserver.dispose();
}
});
$j(elements).find(".tn").unbind("click");

var all_links = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
for (var i = 0 ; i < all_links.length ; i++) {
var href = all_links[i].getAttribute('href');
if (!href || all_links[i].getAttribute('onclick')) continue;
var boolOnClick = true;
if (href.charAt(0) == "/") boolOnClick = false;
else if (href.indexOf("www.cnn.com") != -1 || href.indexOf("blogs.cnn.com") != -1 || href.indexOf("edition.cnn.com") != -1) boolOnClick = false;
if (boolOnClick == true) {
var cleanLink = href.split('&hpt=')[0].split('?hpt=')[0];
all_links[i].setAttribute('onclick', '_vrtrack({ track_url : \'' + cleanLink + '\' })');
}
}

function rightRailPreviewPlayerPostProcessor (elements,model) {
if( window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isFlashInstalled()&&!window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isMobileClient()) {
var thumbChangeObserver = model.thumbnail.subscribe(function(newValue) {
if($j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").length>0) {
$j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").each(function(index){
$j(this).attr("src", newValue);
});
}
else {
if(thumbChangeObserver)thumbChangeObserver.dispose();
}
});
$j(elements).find(".tn").unbind("click");
var vidStreamUrl;
vidStreamUrl = 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr';
callCnnVideo({
key: 'rightRail',
preset: 'right-rail-preview',
markupid: 'nowPlayingThumbnail',
video: 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr',
placement: 'rightRail',
adsection: 'cnn.com_main_homepage_rightrail_muted',
headline: '',
width:'300',
height:'169',
source: 'CNN',
sourceUrl: '',
section: 'largevideo',
videoStreamUrl: vidStreamUrl
});
}
};

Text: The deadliest trip in America?













Immigrants perish on desert trek




Hundreds of immigrants die attempting to traverse the Arizona desert every year. Now investigators are working to help identify their bodies and give answers to desperate family members.

function rightRailPreviewPlayerPostProcessor (elements,model) {
if( window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isFlashInstalled()&&!window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isMobileClient()) {
var thumbChangeObserver = model.thumbnail.subscribe(function(newValue) {
if($j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").length>0) {
$j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").each(function(index){
$j(this).attr("src", newValue);
});
}
else {
if(thumbChangeObserver)thumbChangeObserver.dispose();
}
});
$j(elements).find(".tn").unbind("click");
var vidStreamUrl;
vidStreamUrl = 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr';
callCnnVideo({
key: 'rightRail',
preset: 'right-rail-preview',
markupid: 'nowPlayingThumbnail',
video: 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr',
placement: 'rightRail',
adsection: 'cnn.com_main_homepage_rightrail_muted',
headline: '',
width:'300',
height:'169',
source: 'CNN',
sourceUrl: '',
section: 'largevideo',
videoStreamUrl: vidStreamUrl
});
}
};

Text: LIVE TV





function rightRailPreviewPlayerPostProcessor (elements,model) {
if( window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isFlashInstalled()&&!window.CNNVIDEO_UTILS.isMobileClient()) {
var thumbChangeObserver = model.thumbnail.subscribe(function(newValue) {
if($j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").length>0) {
$j(elements).find(".cnnvideo_wrapper img").each(function(index){
$j(this).attr("src", newValue);
});
}
else {
if(thumbChangeObserver)thumbChangeObserver.dispose();
}
});
$j(elements).find(".tn").unbind("click");
var vidStreamUrl;
vidStreamUrl = 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr';
callCnnVideo({
key: 'rightRail',
preset: 'right-rail-preview',
markupid: 'nowPlayingThumbnail',
video: 'cvptve_prev/muted_cnn_300x169_hprr',
placement: 'rightRail',
adsection: 'cnn.com_main_homepage_rightrail_muted',
headline: '',
width:'300',
height:'169',
source: 'CNN',
sourceUrl: '',
section: 'largevideo',
videoStreamUrl: vidStreamUrl
});
}
};
